Zero Basics

Active Temple Recall
Master Level 1
Description Return to Zero's Temple.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 10, returns to Zero's Temple
Cooldown: 600 sec


Passive Dual Combat
Master Level 1
Description A battle style unique to Alpha and Beta. Tags a Zero on standby, then moves slightly forward.
Right-click to turn Forward Tag ON/OFF.
Level 1 [Tag]: While on standby, use Zero's skills to switch attackers.
Cooldown: 3 sec.
[Assist]: After using Tag to switch, for up to 3 seconds, use Assist for fire support. Cannot be activated while using the previous Assist skill.


Active Divine Aura
Master Level 1
Description Channel the power of the Transcendents to increase the Attack Power, Magic ATT, Attack Speed, Speed, Jump, Defense, Elemental Resistance and Status Resistance of all nearby party members. Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 20, Attack Power: +20, Magic ATT: +20, Attack Speed: +1, Speed: +20, Jump: +10, Defense: +500, All Elemental Resistance: +10%, and All Abnormal Status Resistance: +10%


Active Burst Jump
Master Level 1
Description Compresses time while jumping to extend your jump. Press the up key at the same to move upward.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 5, while jumping, use the jump key to jump certain distance
Can be linked with Burst Step


Active Burst Step
Master Level 1
Description Compress local time to move quickly. Upward Burst Step can't be used immediately after using upward Burst Jump.
Command Lock: Right-click
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 5, press arrow key and then use the skill to move in the corresponding direction
Double-tap an arrow key to move in that direction
Upward Burst Step can't be used immediately after using upward Burst Jump.
Can be used on a ladder or rope. Can be linked with Burst Jump.


Active Rhinne's Protection
Master Level 1
Description Rhinne's protection increases your stats. Using the skill briefly makes Rhinne appear.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 10, the Goddess Rhinne appears.
[Passive Effect: All stats with a direct AP investment increase by 15%.]
Show/hide all levels
Passive Resolution Time
Master Level 5
Description Inherit the Goddess Rhinne's powers, adding them to your own.
Strengthen this skill by collecting Goddess Teardrops.
Level 1 Permanently increases Final Damage by 5%, Critical Rate by 4%, Attack Speed by 1, Strength by 10, Max HP by 3%, and Max Speed by 4
5 Permanently increases Final Damage by 25%, Critical Rate by 20%, Attack Speed by 1, Strength by 50, Max HP by 15%, and Max Speed by 20
Passive Resolution Time
Master Level 5
Description Inherit the Goddess Rhinne's powers, adding them to your own.
Strengthen this skill by collecting Goddess Teardrops.
Level 1 Permanently increases Final Damage by 5%, Critical Rate by 4%, Attack Speed by 1, Strength by 10, Max HP by 3%, and Max Speed by 4
2 Permanently increases Final Damage by 10%, Critical Rate by 8%, Attack Speed by 1, Strength by 20, Max HP by 6%, and Max Speed by 8
3 Permanently increases Final Damage by 15%, Critical Rate by 12%, Attack Speed by 1, Strength by 30, Max HP by 9%, and Max Speed by 12
4 Permanently increases Final Damage by 20%, Critical Rate by 16%, Attack Speed by 1, Strength by 40, Max HP by 12%, and Max Speed by 16
5 Permanently increases Final Damage by 25%, Critical Rate by 20%, Attack Speed by 1, Strength by 50, Max HP by 15%, and Max Speed by 20
Show/hide all levels
Passive Rhinne's Blessing
Master Level 5
Description Receive the Goddess Rhinne's blessings, reducing the damage taken from enemies while ignoring a portion of their defense.
Strengthen this skill by collecting Goddess Teardrops.
Level 1 Incoming damage reduced: 3%, defense ignored: 2%
5 Incoming damage reduced: 15%, defense ignored: 10%
Passive Rhinne's Blessing
Master Level 5
Description Receive the Goddess Rhinne's blessings, reducing the damage taken from enemies while ignoring a portion of their defense.
Strengthen this skill by collecting Goddess Teardrops.
Level 1 Incoming damage reduced: 3%, defense ignored: 2%
2 Incoming damage reduced: 6%, defense ignored: 4%
3 Incoming damage reduced: 9%, defense ignored: 6%
4 Incoming damage reduced: 12%, defense ignored: 8%
5 Incoming damage reduced: 15%, defense ignored: 10%


Passive Doubletime
Level Requirement 100
Master Level 1
Description When you use a skill, the duration is adjusted and the cooldown is reduced. A damage increase effect that can be stacked occurs depending on the attacker.
Level 1 Reduces Zero's attack skill cooldown by 4 seconds (excluding used skill, Transcendent skill, and 5th Job skills).
[Detect]: When Alpha attacks, damage increases by 1% for 20 seconds. Can stack up to 5 times.
[Strength]: When Beta attacks, damage increases by 1% for 20 seconds. Can stack up to 5 times
Effect for [Detect] and [Strength] remains even when tagged.


Active Time Distortion
Level Requirement 110
Master Level 1
Description Summon the power of the Transcendents to distort local time.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 30, Area of Time created for 30 sec
[Enemies within the area]: Every 4 sec, buff cancels, damage taken increases by 25%, and stuns normal monsters
[Party members within the area]: Every 4 sec, Nullify Magic and removes Abnormal Status, Attack Speed: +1
Cooldown: 240 sec


Active Time Holding
Level Requirement 120
Master Level 1
Description Manipulates time to reset your skill cooldowns. Grants invincibility and unlimited Time Force for a short time. Also increases damage for a short time if Zero is Level 200 or above.
Time Holding is not affected by cooldown reset and does not affect other skills that are not affected by cooldown reset.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 10, invincible for 15 sec, reset cooldowns for all skills except those not affected by cooldown reset.
Increase damage by 10% for 90 seconds when Zero is Level 200 or above.
Cooldown: 180 sec


Active Rewind
Level Requirement 140
Master Level 1
Description Capture this moment in your Hourglass. If you get knocked out, time will rewind to the captured moment instead.
Not affected by Cooldown reset.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 10, when you get knocked out you use up the buff instead, restoring all HP and becoming invincible for 2 seconds
Cooldown: 1800 sec


Active The Transcendents' Will
Level Requirement 140
Master Level 1
Description Hones your resolve to ignore certain abnormal status effects. Immune to most abnormal status effects for 3 sec after use. Certain abnormal status effects will still get through.
Level 1 HP Cost: 30, Cooldown: 300 sec


Active Shadow Rain
Level Requirement 160
Master Level 1
Description Alpha and Beta's combination attack. Beta crashes down on the enemy with her Great Sword, stopping them in their tracks. Then Alpha follows up from the shadows, dealing critical damage to all targets.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 50,
[Beta]: Damage: 1600%, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Max Hits: 7
[Alpha]: Damage: 1600%, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Max Hits: 7
Cooldown: 300 sec


Active Focused Time
Level Requirement 200
Master Level 1
Description Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby characters using the power of the Transcendents.
Level 1 Consumes 10 Time Force, increases Attack Power and Magic ATT by 4% for 40 minutes.
Cooldown: 300 sec

Active Shadow Strike
Level Requirement 100
Master Level 10
Description Slash the enemy in front of you. Use this skill with the left or right keys to quickly move to the nearest enemy and attack,
unleashing a strike that penetrates and deals additional damage. Unaffected by attack reflection.
[Skill Requirements]: Piercing Thrust Lv. 1
[Command]: Activate Moon Strike after Piercing Thrust
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 7, Damage: 123%, Number of Attacks: 8, Max Enemies Hit: 8.
[Blade]: Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 220%, Number of Attacks: 1.
10 Time Force Cost: 7, Damage: 195%, Number of Attacks: 8, Max Enemies Hit: 8.
[Blade]: Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 310%, Number of Attacks: 1.

Passive Grand Rolling Cross
Level Requirement 160
Master Level 30
Description An even more powerful Rolling Cross attack. Increase damage and deploy blades that pierce multiple enemies. If activated as an Assist Skill at a certain distance from the enemy, the number of blades will double. Unaffected by attack reflection.
[Skill Requirement]: Rolling Cross Lv. 20
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 13, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 278%, Number of Attacks: 12.
[Blade]: Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 321%, Number of Attacks: 2, Damage Against Normal Enemies: +52%p.
Cooldown: 10 sec
30 Time Force Cost: 13, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 365%, Number of Attacks: 12.
[Blade]: Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 350%, Number of Attacks: 2, Damage Against Normal Enemies: +110%p.
Cooldown: 10 sec
31 Time Force Cost: 13, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 368%, Number of Attacks: 12.
[Blade]: Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 351%, Number of Attacks: 2, Damage Against Normal Enemies: +112%p.
Cooldown: 10 sec
32 Time Force Cost: 13, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 371%, Number of Attacks: 12.
[Blade]: Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 352%, Number of Attacks: 2, Damage Against Normal Enemies: +114%p.
Cooldown: 10 sec

Passive Critical Bind
Level Requirement 185
Master Level 20
Description Beta's attack has a chance to bind boss monsters. Bound enemies will bleed and are more vulnerable to Alpha's attacks. Critical Bind does not share resistance with other incapacitation skills. Using Critical Bind on a boss with an active incapacitation effect whose remaining duration is less than half of Critical Bind's duration will refresh its duration to match that of Critical Bind.
Level 1 Beta's Attack Bind Chance: 1%, Duration: 2 sec. Targets who are not stunned, including normal monsters, will be debuffed for the same amount of time.
Alpha's attacks gain +11% Critical Rate and +10% Critical Damage against targets who are stunned by Critical Bind.
The Bind effect will expire after inflicting damage proportional to the remaining effect duration.
Stunned enemies will resist Critical Bind, and be immune to stunning, for 35 sec. afterwards.
20 Beta's Attack Bind Chance: 10%, Duration: 4 sec. Targets who are not stunned, including normal monsters, will be debuffed for the same amount of time.
Alpha's attacks gain +30% Critical Rate and +20% Critical Damage against targets who are stunned by Critical Bind.
The Bind effect will expire after inflicting damage proportional to the remaining effect duration.
Stunned enemies will resist Critical Bind, and be immune to stunning, for 35 sec. afterwards.

Active Erda Nova
Master Level 25
Description Collect Erda from within yourself and from the surrounding area, then detonate it around your enemies. The Erda of attacked enemies will become disrupted, which will bind their movements. Can deal damage to enemies even when they are under Attack Ignore. Also ignores Attack Reflection.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 156%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 216 sec.
25 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 300%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 120 sec.
30 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 330%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 100 sec.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy
Cooldown: 40 sec
Erda Fountain
Object Summon Duration: 60 sec. Every time enemies in a map with the summoned object are defeated, the Erda released from the enemies condenses around the object.
Defeating 12 or more will release the gathered Erda, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 4
Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Master Level 25
Description Receives the blessing of the Transcendent of Light, Life, and Time. The Spear of Light attacks the boss with the highest HP within range first. Light and Time Blessings are unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5%, Applies Light, Life, and Time Blessing
Light Blessing
Duration: 20 sec
Creates a spear of light when using the attack skill that flies toward enemies in front. Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 260%, Number of Attacks: 4. Remains in place where it sticks, Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 208%, Number of Attacks: 4, Max Continuous Attacks: 5
Max Spears of Light: 7, Spear of Light Cooldown: 2 sec
Life Blessing
Duration: 20 sec
Final Damage: +5%, Number of Debilitating Status Conditions Blocked: 3
Time Blessing
Duration: 31 sec, 100% chance for afterimage of a previous time to remain when using 4th job or lower skills (excluding Beginner Skills), Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 182%, Number of Attacks: 3
Afterimage of skills that triggered Assist for Zero deals 208% damage
Afterimage attack occurs only once per skill
Cooldown: 120 sec

Active Weapon Aura
Master Level 25
Description Infuses your weapon with a portion of your health, granting it a visible aura and temporarily empowering it. The aura wave is unaffected by attack reflection. Affected by effects which reduce cooldown.
Level 1 HP Cost: 10% of Max HP, Ignores 10% Enemy DEF for 82 sec, Final Damage: +1%.
Aura Wave (usable every 5 sec) - Using certain offensive skills will generate waves, inflicting 520% damage on up to 10 enemies, 6 times.
Weapon Aura Prepared: every 180 sec, Max Number Prepared: 2

Active Transcendent Rhinne's Prayer
Master Level 25
Description The prayers of Rhinne, the Transcendent of Time, grant a new ability. Affected by the effects which reduce cooldown.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 30. Reset cooldowns for all skills except the skills that are not affected by cooldown reset.
Duration: 30 sec., Attack Power: +13, Final Damage: +2%.
When Doubletime stacks, gives a buff that creates additional attacks, with 162% damage and 5 additional attacks to enemies you attack with your skills.
Additional hit buff disappears when additional attacks occur, or if Transcendent Rhinne's Prayer ends.
Doubletime and Immune Barrier last for their maximum duration.
Cooldown: 120 sec.
25 Time Force Cost: 30. Reset cooldowns for all skills except the skills that are not affected by cooldown reset.
Duration: 42 sec., Attack Power: +85, Final Damage: +7%.
When Doubletime stacks, gives a buff that creates additional attacks, with 330% damage and 5 additional attacks to enemies you attack with your skills.
Additional hit buff disappears when additional attacks occur, or if Transcendent Rhinne's Prayer ends.

Active Chrono Break
Master Level 25
Description Freeze time, breaking through its limits! When the skill is active, enemies hit are bound, but they cannot be bound again by Chrono Break and other bind skills for 90 sec. To end this skill's effect early, use it again. However, the effects of Chrono Break will not end. The shock dealt at the end of the skill is unaffected by attack ignore and attack reflection.
Level 1 Time Force Cost: 50, Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 218%, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec
Bind Duration: Increases up to 100%, based on initial damage done

Cooldown: 120 sec.

Description Send your weapon to attack enemies with a will of its own. Activated upon successful hits of the Zero character's direct attack skills. Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.
Cyclic Rings are unaffected by attack reflection.

Active Time Piece
Master Level 30
Description Using the power of time from Alpha and Beta, Assist creates Traces of Time after hitting a certain number of times.
These traces can be activated by the Time Crystal whenever the opposite Zero hits, tracking down enemies and attacking them.
The Time Crystal prioritizes targeting the boss with the highest Max HP. Unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 Creates 3 Traces of Time when Assist hits 4 times.
Up to 10 Traces of Time can exist on one map, and are activated by Time Crystal when the opposite Zero's attack hits.
Trace recreation cooldown: 2 seconds
Time Crystal: attacks 4 times with 976% damage
30 Creates 3 Traces of Time when Assist hits 4 times.
Up to 10 Traces of Time can exist on one map, and are activated by Time Crystal when the opposite Zero's attack hits.
Trace recreation cooldown: 2 seconds
Time Crystal: attacks 4 times with 1440% damage

29 Time Force Cost: 15, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 671%, Number of Attacks: 12
Attacks with 3 blades 2 times
[Blade]: Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 1070%, Number of Attacks: 4
When several blades land on a single enemy, Final Damage: -70% starting with the second blade
30 Time Force Cost: 15, Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 680%, Number of Attacks: 12
Attacks with 3 blades 2 times
[Blade]: Max Enemies Hit: 8, Damage: 1090%, Number of Attacks: 4
When several blades land on a single enemy, Final Damage: -70% starting with the second blade


Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
